[16/04/19, 2:30:10 PM] Didige: Collective energy update (April 2019)

There's an important energy in the astrology that's been going on over the past month or so and it seems to be affecting many so I took some time to write about it and some tips on how to approach it. Hope it helps ğŸ™ğŸ™‚ğŸ˜‡ (Pluto, South node conjunction with Saturn in Capricorn). 

You might notice an area (or a few areas) of life where something feels very disempowering. There's an energy of transformation but it doesn't feel easy or pleasant. It's like some truth being revealed straight in the face in its complete messiness/ugliness/powerlessness, which can feel rather unsettling. Like using a plunger in the toilet and having all the dirtiness unclogged, which is good in the long run but doesn't feel very wholesome in the moment (Pluto).

It is highly charged because it's one of those patterns that's been karmically linked to you for a long time through ancestors, previous lifetimes, etc. It might even be so intrinsic to you that until now it just felt like who you are and you never saw this pattern or feelings as clearly as you are now able to (Capricorn). It might be revealed by an event like a break up, death, job loss, finding yourself in a powerless position, boundary violation, etc. or a sudden build-up of inner urgency to be honest with yourself and change something (Pluto).

In the same area, there's also an attitude of surrender and egolessness required which might even be forced by a feeling of helplessness (South node). And there's a simultaneous need to be "responsible" about the way you navigate this messiness or powerlessness. You can't use your "usual coping tactics". The calling is for some higher action and since you're bursting out of your oppressive karmic conditioning, your higher self will feel more available to you than ever before. 

You have to navigate this with some discipline, responsibility, hard work, perseverance. Can't just react immaturely or avoid the lesson (Saturn, Pluto, south node will not let you). Its important to look at what's taking away your power or peace of mind and really inquire about what you can do to help yourself in a mature way. And it's not going to be a quick fix. With Saturn, it's a dedicated sustained effort to commit and work towards whatever that thing is that will eventually leave you feeling truly empowered (Pluto). 

For instance, it may be learning to communicate effectively or learning to respect yourself or learning to set boundaries or committing to discovering yourself or committing to a move or new phase of life or letting go of a toxic person in your life. None of these things happen overnight. They take sustained efforts and commitment. Even though it may feel like a huge task as you start it, you will have some ease, support and even divine grace (Jupiter) as you undertake them. Make sure the action taken is for the highest good of you and others, not out of impulsive/selfish gains at this time (South node will demand spiritual development which is a more selfless than materialistic energy).
